<Name>Murali Krishna Devarakonda<//Name><date>1513623456300<//date><rate>2<//rate><Text>There are many things wrong with this place:
* Not as advertised: I walked in fascinated by their unlimited buffet that's advertised so loudly and prominently on their outside walls - and it's always "not now" (Two nights in a row including a Sunday). They don't bother updating the signs outside.

* Unprofessional: It was open but there was a pile of garbage on the floor and the woman at the counter just stared at me blankly as I recoiled and left
I waited in my car for over 30 minutes, reading reviews and watching a woman with a mop hover around for most of that time- while one family ate.

* Meh:  So I got the "all tiffin combo"- 1 each of dosa, idly, vada, pongal, upma.  Plain dosa was soggy! Clearly they can't be bothered to make a fresh dosa even though the place was practically empty (just one other table occupied). Sambar, as pointed out in another review is  bland and watery- you can taste the powder mixed into water. Chutneys and vada/idly/pongal were fine, but the upma was stale- solid and tasteless!

* Verdict: Try once if you're curious or seriously budget conscious and will eat any desi food regardless of quality. Otherwise... dude,  we're in Sunnyvale, home of dozens of amazing Indian restaurants.< /Text><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Resp>

<username>shanti ayyagari</username><Time>1499582184447</Time><Rate>5</Rate><text>This is my first ever review of any restaurant that I visited to date. My visit to this restaurant was such a serendipity experience that I couldn't help but write my first ever review. I visited with my extended family from India that comprised of my aunts and uncles who were seasoned cooks and connoisseurs at home. It was a Saturday night with unlimited pure vegetarian tiffins thali offer....I was bowled over with the variety of tiffins, immaculate taste and service is an understatement, cuz it was beyond my expectation of good food, ambience and service. It started off with my visit to the washroom to clean my hands to get ready to dig in and I was pleasantly surprised with the cleanliness of the restroom. By the time I was done with washing my hands, a large table was arranged for 11 of us and no sooner than we settled in our seats around the table, piping hot thali filled with punugulu, idli, hot pongal, bisebele bath, vegetable upma, sweet pongal (chakkara pongali) and variety of chatnis welcomed us on our table. The thali was a large stainless steel plate with compartments for different items unlike the usual paper or plastic plates that you encounter in these days in almost all the restaurants. While we were eagerly digging into the thali and relishing the impeccable taste of each item with distinct chatney flavors, piping hot masala dosas, khara podi dosas, plain dosas, pesarattu and utappams started arriving on our table. We wasted no time in devouring those yummy dosas and utappams. Then came pulav with raita and hot & crispy vadas. Mango lassi followed to wash down the delectable tiffins. What made the taste quadrupled was the impeccable service. Everyone of the staff was so friendly and affable that they treated us as one of their own family members by feeding us with so much care and attention. They constantly kept an eye on our table to refill our thalis as soon as we polished it off. As they say, the true taste comes from the service you receive, it was undoubtedly the best service and a surreal experience. What took all of us by surprise was the price tag....it was so affordable and low that we kept wondering how the rest of the bay area restaurants are ripping us off with ordinary food and service. Hats off to the management, service staff and the chefs that gave us a wonderful and wholesome experience in a long time.
Hope the management maintains the quality and standards and they don't lose the chefs and the service staff to the competition. I strongly recommend this place to every food lover in the bay area and around.<//text><Pictures>None<//Pictures><response>None< /response>< GmapID>

My visit was way different than what others have shared.
1) At the counter, the hostess drops the spoon kept in fennel seeds bowl. Picks it up and puts it back in the bowl. I'm never gonna have those fennel seeds, yuk!
2) Food arrived fast, ordered Rava dosa - Sticky, soggy and uncooked. It was so fast, the cook forgot Rava dosa takes long to cook.

4) Chutneys are kept open (for bugs and insects). Had to throw away a cup because one of the insects was too lazy to fly.
5) We should have complained but we were travelling from a long drive and didn't want any drama.

< Review>
Really tasty ribs! The ribs I ordered were meaty, well seasoned,  moist not dry.  I was a pleasant experience eating the ribs.  The potato salad did not disappoint. Again,  well seasoned, good texture not mushy or undercooked.  It's a little different from the normal mayo-based potato salad  but it is good.  Last thing was the green beans. Again, very pleasantly surprised on how good it was.

Overall food is a hit.  Only negative, I felt it was a little over priced at $18.99 for the dinner plate (4 ribs).  I would like 5-6 bones at that price point. But I get it, I'd buy a full rack next time.</Review>
<Pictures>None</Pictures><Resp>None</Resp>< gmap_id>
0x808f945b1f417e6b:0x5c108d4fe17bb3fb<//gmap_id>
</record></dataset><record>
< review>
Take your time... Savor each bite... Let your taste buds share the joy of this food with the rest of your senses... (Wolfing it down is a shame considering all the time, love, and care that goes into this food.)

Ribs (my mouth is watering for more) with green beans (wow, what is the magic seasoning here?) & potato salad (there are no words for a loaded-with-flavor bomb).  Tri tip (juicy and yummy) with candied yams (yes! no skimping on the spices) & potato salad (ditto from above). Wow - all great choices with more sides and dessert to try on our next visit!

Btw- my husband is not a great fan of tri tip because most places make it too dry. But here? I had to keep my fork ready to fend off the poaching!!! Me? I usually cut off the fatty bits. But here? I ate every bit as it literally melted in my mouth. (Hubby was bummed as he usually gets the fatty bits of any bbq from me)

Staff was great - friendly, helpful and full of smiles and laughter! It was like being invited into someone's home for the best bbq! California BBQ ROCKS! - this pastor knows what he's doing...

Oh and the hot bbq sauce is flavorful with just a little kick - just as the pastor described it!</review>

<text>Turns out California CAN do BBQ. Not only is the BBQ in a league of its own, but the sides are also spectacular. They have a sign warning customers that they must buy a meal to get the sides, because the sides have been so popular that people have been running the store out of business.

When you go, make sure to get the potato salad. It is, no exaggeration, the best I have ever had.

A word of caution, it is a bit on the pricey side. For a pork sandwich, side, and tax, I paid just shy of $15. Even so, it's well worth it. You can tell the food is made with genuine love.<//text>< Pictures>

<Text>Found this place near by on my yelp app...I frequent this area often and this is the first time I've seen this place only to learn it just open 6 months ago. Break down:

Had the bishop platter which is a sample of the brisket, rib, mild or hot link and chicken and two sides I had the bake beans and fries.

The brisket was tender but kind tasted old....give 3/5 only cause I think it can get better

Mild (beef)link 5/5 not spice at all so if you want a kick go with the hot (pork)link

Chicken was my favorite very tender and juicy perfectly cook with the right amount of sauce. 5/5

Rib 5/5 very tender falling off the bone and juicy.

Overall 5/5 will definitely be back around.

Would be 10/5 if they had rib tips :0) since I am from Chicago< /Text>< Time>

<time>1584580627714< /time><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
The Pad has been my home away from home for the last 10 years. It has always been well kept, well ventilated, and well attended. The atmosphere manages to be zen and cheerful at the same time and class playlists are always on point--somehow both chill and trendy, not too woo-woo, and never overbearing.

All of that aside, it's the quality of the teaching and the warmth of the teachers--every single one fo them--that has kept me coming back to The Pad for a decade. They each bring a special quality to their particular class, whether it's a good sweat, focus on the breath, proper alignment, or a deep sense of empathy and self-acceptance that draws us all to the principles of yoga.

As we all try to stay sane during this difficult time of social distancing, I encourage everyone to support this very worthy small business and sign up for virtual live classes. And when it's all over, go down to the corner of Gough/Union and take a class in person. Thank you for listening to my Ted Talk.</review>

<time>1401633027099<//time><Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
My friend brought me here for power yoga recently and I honestly loved it. I don't generally like yoga, either.

Pros:
- Beautiful space, well lit, kept at a decently warm temperature but with plenty of movement so it's not stuffy
- The power yoga class involves movement, strength, and flexibility in almost equal portions. It has a simultaneously calming and energizing effect. I haven't experienced that before but it was great.
- The teacher is very gentle about corrections in form, which lets you enjoy the class even if you're a beginner (she will correct you, but not loudly or anything)

Cons:
- The mats are sweaty and gross - spraying them with water at the end does not constitute cleaning in my view< /review>

< text>
I've been going to the Shell station at Prather since I began cycling some years ago. I had been a runner but my knees gave out, and I had to try something different. There are quite a few routes for those of us who cycle, but one of my favorite is from my house in Old Town up to Prather via Auberry Road. The climb is worthy, and I do it every Friday. Sometimes on the weekend. It's a 48 mile round trip. Everybody at the Shell station is friendly and nice to cyclists and anybody who walks through the door. They'll answer questions, and it's like going back to Mayberry. There's good food and a selection of just about anything. The management has done some fantastic landscaping that makes it a real jewel for the community. And they sell gas. I've stopped there a number of times on my way to Shaver Lake.<//text>
